\subsection{Detailed Description}
This is a general header that includes C language support.

This function converts a string between encodings in one pass, returning a string that must be freed with \mbox{\hyperlink{_s_d_l__stdinc_8h_a0e4ade894d550ada1fa19dc2d46e88b8}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+free()}} or N\+U\+LL on error. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__stdinc_8h_a3e2b095edf06856900b16babe77809cf}\label{_s_d_l__stdinc_8h_a3e2b095edf06856900b16babe77809cf}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Memory\+Functions()}{SDL\_SetMemoryFunctions()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{begin__code_8h_aa4c7a931f4a968f818b2a1b10a432185}{D\+E\+C\+L\+S\+P\+EC}} int \mbox{\hyperlink{begin__code_8h_a81faf4ba0455dc75f2e0507eddb79401}{S\+D\+L\+C\+A\+LL}} S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Memory\+Functions (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_s_d_l__stdinc_8h_a9c080fa72a520c3fb9cc547277d131b2}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+malloc\+\_\+func}}}]{malloc\+\_\+func,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_s_d_l__stdinc_8h_a49ece773aefa50992c057d6bde28fece}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+calloc\+\_\+func}}}]{calloc\+\_\+func,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_s_d_l__stdinc_8h_a28010cd6bfed0bdeab394f864cfc05bc}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+realloc\+\_\+func}}}]{realloc\+\_\+func,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_s_d_l__stdinc_8h_a38b6aadadc8fa09f817ebbd0567b99fb}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+free\+\_\+func}}}]{free\+\_\+func }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Replace S\+DL\textquotesingle{}s memory allocation functions with a custom set. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If you are replacing S\+DL\textquotesingle{}s memory functions, you should call \mbox{\hyperlink{_s_d_l__stdinc_8h_a853b94eb0e35bf92556807e23d445bc0}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Num\+Allocations()}} and be very careful if it returns non-\/zero. That means that your free function will be called with memory allocated by the previous memory allocation functions. 
\end{DoxyNote}
